<script>
'use strict';

// ============================================
// AUTH
// ============================================
(function() {
    const u = sessionStorage.getItem('rk_username') || 'Admin';
    document.getElementById('uname').textContent   = u;
    document.getElementById('uavatar').textContent = u.substring(0,2).toUpperCase();
})();


// ============================================
// HELPERS
// ============================================
function escHtml(s) {
    return String(s)
        .replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;')
        .replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;');
}

function nowStr() {
    const d = new Date();
    const months = ['Jan','Feb','Mar','Apr','Mei','Jun','Jul','Agu','Sep','Okt','Nov','Des'];
    return d.getDate()+' '+months[d.getMonth()]+' '+d.getFullYear();
}

function fmtDate(iso) {
    if (!iso) return '—';
    const [y,m,d] = iso.split('-');
    const months = ['Jan','Feb','Mar','Apr','Mei','Jun','Jul','Agu','Sep','Okt','Nov','Des'];
    return +d+' '+months[+m-1]+' '+y;
}

function showToast(msg, type='success') {
    const colors = { success:'#15803D', warning:'#B45309', danger:'#B91C1C' };
    const t  = document.getElementById('toast');
    const dt = document.getElementById('toastDot');
    dt.style.background = colors[type] || '#888';
    document.getElementById('toastMsg').textContent = msg;
    t.className = 'toast '+type+' show';
    clearTimeout(t._timer);
    t._timer = setTimeout(()=>t.classList.remove('show'), 3500);
}

function openModal(id) { document.getElementById(id).classList.add('open'); }
function closeModal(id){ document.getElementById(id).classList.remove('open'); }

// close on backdrop
['draftModal','publishModal','deleteDraftModal','logoutModal',
 'galDraftModal','galPublishModal','galDeleteModal','galEditModal','galLightbox'
].forEach(id => {
    document.getElementById(id).addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        if (e.target === this) this.classList.remove('open');
    });
});


// ============================================
// ARTIKEL STATE
// ============================================
let drafts    = [];
let editingId = null;
let deletingId = null;
let pubCount  = 45;

function renderDraftList() {
    const count = drafts.length;
    document.getElementById('draftCountLabel').textContent = count+' draft';
    document.getElementById('statDraft').textContent = count;

    const container = document.getElementById('draftListContainer');
    if (count === 0) {
        container.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state"><svg class="empty-icon" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M19 21H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11l5 5v11a2 2 0 0 1-2 2z"/></svg><div class="empty-text">Belum ada draft tersimpan.</div></div>`;
    } else {
        container.innerHTML = `<div style="padding:.5rem 1.5rem 1rem">`+
            drafts.map(d=>`
                <div class="draft-item" onclick="loadDraft(${d.id})">
                    <div class="draft-item-row">
                        <div><div class="draft-item-title">${escHtml(d.judul)}</div><div class="draft-item-meta">${d.tgl} &middot; ${escHtml(d.kat)}</div></div>
                        <button class="draft-del-btn" onclick="openDeleteDraftModal(event,${d.id})">Hapus</button>
                    </div>
                    <div class="edit-hint">↵ Klik untuk lanjut edit</div>
                </div>`).join('')+`</div>`;
    }

    const db = document.getElementById('dashboardDraftList');
    if (count === 0) {
        db.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state" style="padding:1.5rem"><div class="empty-text">Belum ada draft tersimpan.</div></div>`;
    } else {
        db.innerHTML = drafts.map(d=>`
            <div class="article-item">
                <div class="article-name">${escHtml(d.judul)}</div>
                <div class="article-meta">${d.tgl} &middot; ${escHtml(d.kat)}</div>
                <span class="status-badge badge-draft">Draft</span>
            </div>`).join('');
    }
}

function loadDraft(id) {
    const d = drafts.find(x=>x.id===id); if(!d) return;
    document.getElementById('artJudul').value    = d.judul;
    document.getElementById('artKategori').value = d.kat;
    document.getElementById('artIsi').innerHTML  = d.isi;
    document.getElementById('artFotoTxt').textContent = d.foto ? '✓ '+d.foto : 'Klik untuk pilih gambar sampul';
    document.getElementById('editorModeLabel').textContent = 'Edit Draft';
    document.getElementById('editModeBannerText').textContent = 'Sedang mengedit: "'+d.judul+'"';
    document.getElementById('editModeBanner').classList.add('visible');
    editingId = id;
    showSectionByName('artikel');
    showToast('Draft "'+d.judul+'" dimuat ke editor.','warning');
}

function resetEditor() {
    document.getElementById('artJudul').value    = '';
    document.getElementById('artIsi').innerHTML  = '';
    document.getElementById('artFoto').value     = '';
    document.getElementById('artFotoTxt').textContent = 'Klik untuk pilih gambar sampul';
    document.getElementById('editorModeLabel').textContent = 'Artikel baru';
    document.getElementById('editModeBanner').classList.remove('visible');
    editingId = null;
}

function openDraftModal() {
    const judul = document.getElementById('artJudul').value.trim();
    if (!judul) { showToast('Judul artikel wajib diisi.','warning'); return; }
    const kat = document.getElementById('artKategori').value;
    document.getElementById('draftModalJudul').textContent = judul;
    document.getElementById('draftModalMeta').textContent  = kat+' · Draft';
    openModal('draftModal');
}
function closeDraftModal() { closeModal('draftModal'); }

function confirmSaveDraft() {
    const judul = document.getElementById('artJudul').value.trim();
    const kat   = document.getElementById('artKategori').value;
    const isi   = document.getElementById('artIsi').innerHTML;
    const foto  = document.getElementById('artFoto').files[0]?.name || null;
    if (editingId !== null) {
        const idx = drafts.findIndex(x=>x.id===editingId);
        if (idx > -1) drafts[idx] = {...drafts[idx], judul, kat, isi, foto, tgl: nowStr()};
    } else {
        drafts.push({ id: Date.now(), judul, kat, isi, foto, tgl: nowStr() });
    }
    closeDraftModal(); resetEditor(); renderDraftList();
    showToast('Draft "'+judul+'" berhasil disimpan.','warning');
}

function openDeleteDraftModal(e, id) {
    e.stopPropagation();
    const d = drafts.find(x=>x.id===id); if(!d) return;
    deletingId = id;
    document.getElementById('deleteDraftModalJudul').textContent = d.judul;
    document.getElementById('deleteDraftModalMeta').textContent  = d.tgl+' · '+d.kat;
    openModal('deleteDraftModal');
}
function closeDeleteDraftModal() { closeModal('deleteDraftModal'); deletingId=null; }

function confirmDeleteDraft() {
    const d = drafts.find(x=>x.id===deletingId);
    drafts = drafts.filter(x=>x.id!==deletingId);
    if (editingId === deletingId) resetEditor();
    closeDeleteDraftModal(); renderDraftList();
    showToast('Draft "'+(d?d.judul:'')+'" dihapus.','danger');
}

function openPublishModal() {
    const judul = document.getElementById('artJudul').value.trim();
    const isi   = document.getElementById('artIsi').innerText.trim();
    if (!judul) { showToast('Judul artikel wajib diisi.','warning'); return; }
    if (!isi)   { showToast('Isi artikel tidak boleh kosong.','warning'); return; }
    const kat = document.getElementById('artKategori').value;
    document.getElementById('publishModalJudul').textContent = judul;
    document.getElementById('publishModalMeta').textContent  = kat+' · '+nowStr();
    openModal('publishModal');
}
function closePublishModal() { closeModal('publishModal'); }

function confirmPublish() {
    const judul = document.getElementById('artJudul').value.trim();
    const kat   = document.getElementById('artKategori').value;
    if (editingId !== null) { drafts = drafts.filter(x=>x.id!==editingId); renderDraftList(); }
    pubCount++;
    document.getElementById('pubCountLabel').textContent = pubCount+' artikel';
    document.getElementById('statPub').textContent = pubCount;
    const pubContainer = document.getElementById('publishedListContainer');
    const ni = document.createElement('div'); ni.className='article-item';
    ni.innerHTML = `<div class="article-name">${escHtml(judul)}</div><div class="article-meta">${nowStr()} &middot; ${escHtml(kat)}</div><span class="status-badge badge-published">Terbit</span>`;
    pubContainer.insertBefore(ni, pubContainer.firstChild);
    closePublishModal(); resetEditor();
    showToast('Artikel "'+judul+'" berhasil diterbitkan!','success');
}

function fmt(cmd) { document.execCommand(cmd,false,null); document.getElementById('artIsi').focus(); }

document.getElementById('artFoto').addEventListener('change', function() {
    const f = this.files[0];
    const allowed = ['image/jpeg','image/jpg','image/png','image/webp'];
    if (f && !allowed.includes(f.type)) { showToast('Format tidak didukung.','danger'); this.value=''; return; }
    if (f && f.size > 5*1024*1024) { showToast('File terlalu besar (maks 5MB).','danger'); this.value=''; return; }
    if (f) document.getElementById('artFotoTxt').textContent = '✓ '+f.name;
});

const ICON_CHECK = `<svg class="empty-icon" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M22 11.08V12a10 10 0 1 1-5.93-9.14"/><polyline points="22 4 12 14.01 9 11.01"/></svg>`;

function renderKomentar() {
    const pending = comments.filter(c=>c.status==='pending');
    const count   = pending.length;
    const badge   = document.getElementById('badgeCmt');
    badge.textContent   = count;
    badge.style.display = count ? 'inline-flex' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('statCmt').textContent = count;
    document.getElementById('cntCmt').textContent  = count+' menunggu';

    const tbody = document.getElementById('komentarTable');
    tbody.innerHTML = pending.length
        ? pending.map(c=>`<tr><td><div class="td-name">${escHtml(c.nama)}</div></td><td style="max-width:220px;font-size:.82rem;color:var(--gray)">${escHtml(c.teks)}</td><td><div class="td-sub">${escHtml(c.artikel)}</div></td><td><div class="td-sub">${c.tgl}</div></td><td><span class="status-badge badge-pending">Pending</span></td><td><button class="action-btn approve" onclick="approveKomentar(${c.id})">Setujui</button><button class="action-btn reject" onclick="rejectKomentar(${c.id})">Tolak</button></td></tr>`).join('')
        : `<tr><td colspan="6"><div class="empty-state">${ICON_CHECK}<div class="empty-text">Semua komentar sudah dimoderasi.</div></div></td></tr>`;

    const pv = document.getElementById('previewCmt');
    pv.innerHTML = pending.length
        ? `<table class="data-table"><thead><tr><th>Pengirim</th><th>Komentar</th><th>Status</th><th>Aksi</th></tr></thead><tbody>${pending.slice(0,2).map(c=>`<tr><td><div class="td-name">${escHtml(c.nama)}</div><div class="td-sub">${c.tgl}</div></td><td style="font-size:.82rem;color:var(--gray)">${escHtml(c.teks.substring(0,55))}...</td><td><span class="status-badge badge-pending">Pending</span></td><td><button class="action-btn approve" onclick="approveKomentar(${c.id})">Setujui</button><button class="action-btn reject" onclick="rejectKomentar(${c.id})">Tolak</button></td></tr>`).join('')}</tbody></table>`
        : `<div class="empty-state">${ICON_CHECK}<div class="empty-text">Tidak ada komentar pending.</div></div>`;
}

function approveKomentar(id) { const c=comments.find(x=>x.id===id); if(c){c.status='approved';renderKomentar();showToast('Komentar '+c.nama+' disetujui.','success');} }
function rejectKomentar(id)  { const c=comments.find(x=>x.id===id); if(c){c.status='rejected';renderKomentar();showToast('Komentar ditolak.','danger');} }

    const badge   = document.getElementById('badgeFoto');

    badge.style.display = count ? 'inline-flex' : 'none';

    document.getElementById('cntFoto').textContent  = count+' menunggu';

        : `<tr><td colspan="5"><div class="empty-state">${ICON_CHECK}<div class="empty-text">Tidak ada foto pending.</div></div></td></tr>`;
}

function rejectFoto(id)  { const p=photos.find(x=>x.id===id); if(p){p.status='rejected';renderFoto();showToast('Foto ditolak.','danger');} }

// galEntries: array of objects
// { id, judul, kat, tgl, desk, dataUrls[], status, uploadTgl, gradIdx }

let galGridVisible = true;
let galPubCount    = 6;

// staged files (FileList equivalent) stored as data URLs before submit
let galStagedFiles = []; // [{name, dataUrl, size}]

// Sample published entries (seed data)
const SEED_GAL = [

galEntries = [...SEED_GAL];

function galCountPublished() { return galEntries.filter(e=>e.status==='published').length; }
function galCountDraft()     { return galEntries.filter(e=>e.status==='draft').length; }
function galCountFoto()      { return galEntries.reduce((s,e)=>s+e.dataUrls.length,0)+galTotalFoto; }

function updateGalStats() {
    document.getElementById('galStatDraft').textContent = galCountDraft();
    document.getElementById('galStatPub').textContent   = galCountPublished();
    document.getElementById('galStatFoto').textContent  = galCountFoto();
    document.getElementById('galDraftCountLabel').textContent = galCountDraft()+' draft';
}

// ---- File input & drag-drop ----
const galDropZone = document.getElementById('galDropZone');
const galFotoInput = document.getElementById('galFotoInput');

galFotoInput.addEventListener('change', function() {
    handleGalFiles(Array.from(this.files));
});

galDropZone.addEventListener('dragover', e => { e.preventDefault(); galDropZone.classList.add('dragover'); });
galDropZone.addEventListener('dragleave', () => galDropZone.classList.remove('dragover'));
galDropZone.addEventListener('drop', e => {
    e.preventDefault(); galDropZone.classList.remove('dragover');
    handleGalFiles(Array.from(e.dataTransfer.files));
});

function handleGalFiles(files) {
    const allowed  = ['image/jpeg','image/jpg','image/png','image/webp'];
    const errEl    = document.getElementById('galErr');
    errEl.style.display = 'none';

    for (const f of files) {
        if (!allowed.includes(f.type)) {
            errEl.textContent   = '"'+f.name+'" bukan format yang didukung (JPG/PNG/WEBP).';
            errEl.style.display = 'block'; return;
        }
        if (f.size > 5*1024*1024) {
            errEl.textContent   = '"'+f.name+'" melebihi batas 5MB.';
            errEl.style.display = 'block'; return;
        }
    }

    // Read files as data URLs
    files.forEach(f => {
        const reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = ev => {
            galStagedFiles.push({ name: f.name, dataUrl: ev.target.result, size: f.size });
            renderGalPreviewStrip();
        };
        reader.readAsDataURL(f);
    });
}

function renderGalPreviewStrip() {
    const strip    = document.getElementById('galPreviewStrip');
    const countEl  = document.getElementById('galPreviewCount');
    if (galStagedFiles.length === 0) {
        strip.style.display  = 'none';
        countEl.style.display = 'none';
        return;
    }
    strip.style.display  = 'flex';
    countEl.style.display = 'block';
    countEl.textContent   = galStagedFiles.length+' foto dipilih';
    strip.innerHTML = galStagedFiles.map((f,i) => `
        <div class="gal-preview-thumb">
            <img src="${f.dataUrl}" alt="${escHtml(f.name)}">
            <button class="gal-preview-thumb-del" onclick="removeGalStagedFile(${i})" title="Hapus">✕</button>
        </div>`).join('');
}

function removeGalStagedFile(idx) {
    galStagedFiles.splice(idx,1);
    renderGalPreviewStrip();
}

// ---- Editor reset ----
function resetGalEditor() {
    document.getElementById('galJudul').value         = '';
    document.getElementById('galKategori').value      = 'Seminar';
    document.getElementById('galTglKegiatan').value   = '';
    document.getElementById('galDeskripsi').value     = '';
    document.getElementById('galEditorLabel').textContent = 'Entri baru';
    document.getElementById('galEditBanner').classList.remove('visible');
    document.getElementById('galErr').style.display   = 'none';
    galStagedFiles = [];
    galFotoInput.value = '';
    renderGalPreviewStrip();
    galEditingId = null;
}

// ---- Load galeri item ke editor ----
function loadGalEntry(id) {
    const e = galEntries.find(x=>x.id===id); if(!e) return;
    document.getElementById('galJudul').value       = e.judul;
    document.getElementById('galKategori').value    = e.kat;
    document.getElementById('galTglKegiatan').value = e.tgl;
    document.getElementById('galDeskripsi').value   = e.desk;
    document.getElementById('galEditorLabel').textContent = 'Edit Entri';
    document.getElementById('galEditBannerText').textContent = 'Sedang mengedit: "'+e.judul+'"';
    document.getElementById('galEditBanner').classList.add('visible');
    galStagedFiles = e.dataUrls.map(u=>({ name:'existing', dataUrl:u, size:0 }));
    renderGalPreviewStrip();
    galEditingId = id;
    showSectionByName('galeri');
    showToast('Entri "'+e.judul+'" dimuat ke editor.','warning');
}

// ---- Open DRAFT MODAL ----
function openGalDraftModal() {
    const judul = document.getElementById('galJudul').value.trim();
    if (!judul) { showToast('Judul album wajib diisi.','warning'); return; }
    const kat = document.getElementById('galKategori').value;
    const tgl = document.getElementById('galTglKegiatan').value;
    document.getElementById('galDraftModalJudul').textContent = judul;
    document.getElementById('galDraftModalMeta').textContent  = kat+(tgl?' · '+fmtDate(tgl):'')+(galStagedFiles.length?' · '+galStagedFiles.length+' foto':'');
    // Thumb preview
    const thumbWrap = document.getElementById('galDraftModalThumb');
    if (galStagedFiles.length > 0) {
        thumbWrap.innerHTML = `<img src="${galStagedFiles[0].dataUrl}" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover">`;
    } else {
        thumbWrap.innerHTML = `<svg width="32" height="32" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.25" style="color:var(--border)"><rect x="3" y="3" width="18" height="18" rx="2"/><circle cx="8.5" cy="8.5" r="1.5"/><path d="m21 15-5-5L5 21"/></svg>`;
    }
    openModal('galDraftModal');
}

function confirmGalDraft() {
    const judul = document.getElementById('galJudul').value.trim();
    const kat   = document.getElementById('galKategori').value;
    const tgl   = document.getElementById('galTglKegiatan').value;
    const desk  = document.getElementById('galDeskripsi').value;
    const dataUrls = galStagedFiles.map(f=>f.dataUrl);

    if (galEditingId !== null) {
        const idx = galEntries.findIndex(x=>x.id===galEditingId);
        if (idx > -1) galEntries[idx] = { ...galEntries[idx], judul, kat, tgl, desk, dataUrls, status:'draft', uploadTgl: nowStr() };
    } else {
        galEntries.push({ id: Date.now(), judul, kat, tgl, desk, dataUrls, status:'draft', uploadTgl: nowStr(), gradIdx: Math.floor(Math.random()*GAL_GRADIENTS.length) });
    }
    closeModal('galDraftModal');
    resetGalEditor();
    renderGalDraftList();
    renderGalPubGrid();
    updateGalStats();
    showToast('Draft galeri "'+judul+'" disimpan.','warning');
}

// ---- Open PUBLISH MODAL ----
function openGalPublishModal() {
    const judul = document.getElementById('galJudul').value.trim();
    if (!judul) { showToast('Judul album wajib diisi.','warning'); return; }
    if (galStagedFiles.length === 0) { showToast('Pilih minimal 1 foto.','warning'); return; }
    const kat = document.getElementById('galKategori').value;
    const tgl = document.getElementById('galTglKegiatan').value;
    document.getElementById('galPublishModalJudul').textContent = judul;
    document.getElementById('galPublishModalMeta').textContent  = kat+(tgl?' · '+fmtDate(tgl):'')+ ' · '+galStagedFiles.length+' foto';
    const thumbWrap = document.getElementById('galPublishModalThumb');
    if (galStagedFiles.length > 0) {
        thumbWrap.innerHTML = `<img src="${galStagedFiles[0].dataUrl}" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover">`;
    }
    openModal('galPublishModal');
}

function confirmGalPublish() {
    const judul = document.getElementById('galJudul').value.trim();
    const kat   = document.getElementById('galKategori').value;
    const tgl   = document.getElementById('galTglKegiatan').value;
    const desk  = document.getElementById('galDeskripsi').value;
    const dataUrls = galStagedFiles.map(f=>f.dataUrl);

    if (galEditingId !== null) {
        const idx = galEntries.findIndex(x=>x.id===galEditingId);
        if (idx > -1) galEntries[idx] = { ...galEntries[idx], judul, kat, tgl, desk, dataUrls, status:'published', uploadTgl: nowStr() };
    } else {
        galEntries.push({ id: Date.now(), judul, kat, tgl, desk, dataUrls, status:'published', uploadTgl: nowStr(), gradIdx: Math.floor(Math.random()*GAL_GRADIENTS.length) });
    }
    closeModal('galPublishModal');
    resetGalEditor();
    renderGalDraftList();
    renderGalPubGrid();
    updateGalStats();
    showToast('Album "'+judul+'" berhasil diterbitkan ke galeri!','success');
}

// ---- Hapus galeri ----
function openGalDeleteModal(id) {
    const e = galEntries.find(x=>x.id===id); if(!e) return;
    galDeletingId = id;
    document.getElementById('galDeleteModalJudul').textContent = e.judul;
    document.getElementById('galDeleteModalMeta').textContent  = e.kat+' · '+fmtDate(e.tgl)+(e.dataUrls.length?' · '+e.dataUrls.length+' foto':'');
    openModal('galDeleteModal');
}

function confirmGalDelete() {
    const e = galEntries.find(x=>x.id===galDeletingId);
    galEntries = galEntries.filter(x=>x.id!==galDeletingId);
    if (galEditingId === galDeletingId) resetGalEditor();
    closeModal('galDeleteModal'); galDeletingId=null;
    renderGalDraftList(); renderGalPubGrid(); updateGalStats();
    closeLightbox();
    showToast('Entri "'+(e?e.judul:'')+'" dihapus.','danger');
}

// ---- Edit inline modal ----
function openGalEditModal(id) {
    const e = galEntries.find(x=>x.id===id); if(!e) return;
    galDeletingId = id; // reuse for edit target
    document.getElementById('galEditJudul').value   = e.judul;
    document.getElementById('galEditKategori').value= e.kat;
    document.getElementById('galEditTgl').value     = e.tgl;
    document.getElementById('galEditDesk').value    = e.desk;
    openModal('galEditModal');
}

function confirmGalEdit() {
    const id   = galDeletingId;
    const idx  = galEntries.findIndex(x=>x.id===id);
    if (idx < 0) { closeModal('galEditModal'); return; }
    galEntries[idx].judul = document.getElementById('galEditJudul').value.trim() || galEntries[idx].judul;
    galEntries[idx].kat   = document.getElementById('galEditKategori').value;
    galEntries[idx].tgl   = document.getElementById('galEditTgl').value;
    galEntries[idx].desk  = document.getElementById('galEditDesk').value;
    closeModal('galEditModal');
    renderGalDraftList(); renderGalPubGrid(); updateGalStats();
    // Refresh lightbox if open
    if (document.getElementById('galLightbox').classList.contains('open')) {
        openLightbox(id);
    }
    showToast('Entri "'+galEntries[idx].judul+'" diperbarui.','warning');
}

// ---- Publish dari draft list ----
function publishGalFromDraft(id) {
    const idx = galEntries.findIndex(x=>x.id===id); if(idx<0) return;
    galEntries[idx].status = 'published';
    renderGalDraftList(); renderGalPubGrid(); updateGalStats();
    showToast('Album "'+galEntries[idx].judul+'" diterbitkan.','success');
}

// ---- RENDER: Draft list ----
function renderGalDraftList() {
    const all = galEntries.filter(e=>e.status==='draft');
    const list = galActiveFilterDraft === 'all' ? all : all.filter(e=>e.kat===galActiveFilterDraft);
    const container = document.getElementById('galDraftList');

    if (list.length === 0) {
        container.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state"><svg class="empty-icon" style="color:var(--muted)" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><rect x="3" y="3" width="18" height="18" rx="2"/><circle cx="8.5" cy="8.5" r="1.5"/><path d="m21 15-5-5L5 21"/></svg><div class="empty-text">Belum ada draft galeri.</div></div>`;
        return;
    }

    container.innerHTML = list.map(e => {
        const thumbHtml = e.dataUrls.length
            ? `<img src="${e.dataUrls[0]}" alt="${escHtml(e.judul)}">`
            : `<div class="gal-item-thumb-placeholder" style="background:${GAL_GRADIENTS[e.gradIdx]}"></div>`;
        const countBadge = e.dataUrls.length > 1
            ? `<div class="gal-count-badge">${e.dataUrls.length}</div>` : '';
        return `
            <div class="gal-item" onclick="openLightbox(${e.id})">
                <div class="gal-item-thumb">${thumbHtml}${countBadge}</div>
                <div class="gal-item-info">
                    <div class="gal-item-title">${escHtml(e.judul)}</div>
                    <div class="gal-item-meta">${escHtml(e.kat)} · ${fmtDate(e.tgl) || '—'}</div>
                    <div style="margin-top:.3rem"><span class="status-badge badge-draft">Draft</span></div>
                </div>
                <div class="gal-item-actions">
                    <button class="gal-action-btn pub" onclick="event.stopPropagation();publishGalFromDraft(${e.id})">Terbitkan</button>
                    <button class="gal-action-btn" onclick="event.stopPropagation();loadGalEntry(${e.id})">Edit</button>
                    <button class="gal-action-btn del" onclick="event.stopPropagation();openGalDeleteModal(${e.id})">Hapus</button>
                </div>
            </div>`;
    }).join('');
}

// ---- RENDER: Published grid ----
function renderGalPubGrid() {
    const all  = galEntries.filter(e=>e.status==='published');
    const list = galActiveFilterPub === 'all' ? all : all.filter(e=>e.kat===galActiveFilterPub);
    const grid = document.getElementById('galPubGrid');
    const emptyEl = document.getElementById('galPubEmpty');

    if (list.length === 0) {
        grid.innerHTML = '';
        emptyEl.style.display = 'block';
    } else {
        emptyEl.style.display = 'none';
        grid.innerHTML = list.map(e => {
            const bg = e.dataUrls.length ? '' : `style="background:${GAL_GRADIENTS[e.gradIdx]}"`;
            const imgHtml = e.dataUrls.length
                ? `<img src="${e.dataUrls[0]}" alt="${escHtml(e.judul)}">`
                : `<div class="gal-grid-item-placeholder" ${bg}></div>`;
            return `
                <div class="gal-grid-item" onclick="openLightbox(${e.id})">
                    ${imgHtml}
                    <div class="gal-grid-overlay">
                        <div class="gal-grid-item-label">${escHtml(e.judul)}</div>
                    </div>
                    ${e.dataUrls.length > 1 ? `<div class="gal-count-badge" style="position:absolute;top:5px;right:5px;z-index:1">${e.dataUrls.length}</div>` : ''}
                </div>`;
        }).join('');
    }
}

// ---- Filter tabs ----
function setGalFilter(type, val, btn) {
    if (type === 'draft') {
        galActiveFilterDraft = val;
        document.querySelectorAll('#galDraftFilterTabs .gal-tab').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
    } else {
        galActiveFilterPub = val;
        // find parent tabs
        btn.closest('.gal-filter-tabs').querySelectorAll('.gal-tab').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
    }
    btn.classList.add('active');
    if (type === 'draft') renderGalDraftList();
    else renderGalPubGrid();
}

// ---- Toggle grid visibility ----
function toggleGalGrid() {
    galGridVisible = !galGridVisible;
    const wrap = document.getElementById('galPubGridWrap');
    wrap.style.display = galGridVisible ? 'block' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('galGridToggleLabel').textContent = galGridVisible ? 'Sembunyikan' : 'Tampilkan';
}


// ============================================
// LIGHTBOX
// ============================================
let lbCurrentEntry = null;
let lbCurrentIdx   = 0;

function openLightbox(id) {
    const e = galEntries.find(x=>x.id===id); if(!e) return;
    lbCurrentEntry = e;
    lbCurrentIdx   = 0;
    renderLightbox();
    openModal('galLightbox');
}

function closeLightbox() { closeModal('galLightbox'); }

function renderLightbox() {
    const e = lbCurrentEntry;
    document.getElementById('lbTitle').textContent     = e.judul;
    document.getElementById('lbKategori').textContent  = e.kat;
    document.getElementById('lbTgl').textContent       = fmtDate(e.tgl) || '—';
    document.getElementById('lbDesk').textContent      = e.desk || '—';
    document.getElementById('lbTglUpload').textContent = e.uploadTgl || nowStr();

    // Status badge
    const statusEl = document.getElementById('lbStatus');
    statusEl.innerHTML = e.status === 'published'
        ? `<span class="status-badge badge-published">Terbit</span>`
        : `<span class="status-badge badge-draft">Draft</span>`;

    // Main image
    const mainWrap = document.getElementById('lbMainImgWrap');
    const hasImgs  = e.dataUrls.length > 0;
    if (hasImgs) {
        // Ensure index in range
        if (lbCurrentIdx >= e.dataUrls.length) lbCurrentIdx = 0;
        mainWrap.innerHTML = `
            <img src="${e.dataUrls[lbCurrentIdx]}" alt="${escHtml(e.judul)}" style="max-width:100%;max-height:100%;object-fit:contain">
            <button class="lightbox-nav prev" id="lbPrev" onclick="lbNav(-1)">
                <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="15 18 9 12 15 6"/></svg>
            </button>
            <button class="lightbox-nav next" id="lbNext" onclick="lbNav(1)">
                <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="9 18 15 12 9 6"/></svg>
            </button>`;
        // Hide nav if single
        if (e.dataUrls.length <= 1) {
            mainWrap.querySelector('.prev').style.display = 'none';
            mainWrap.querySelector('.next').style.display = 'none';
        }
    } else {
        mainWrap.innerHTML = `
            <div class="lightbox-main-placeholder">
                <div style="width:80px;height:80px;border-radius:12px;${GAL_GRADIENTS[e.gradIdx].includes('gradient') ? 'background:'+GAL_GRADIENTS[e.gradIdx] : ''}"></div>
                <span style="font-size:.78rem;margin-top:.5rem">Tidak ada foto</span>
            </div>
            <button class="lightbox-nav prev" style="display:none"></button>
            <button class="lightbox-nav next" style="display:none"></button>`;
    }

    // Strip
    const strip = document.getElementById('lbStrip');
    if (hasImgs && e.dataUrls.length > 1) {
        strip.innerHTML = e.dataUrls.map((u,i)=>
            `<div class="lightbox-strip-thumb ${i===lbCurrentIdx?'active':''}" onclick="lbGoTo(${i})">
                <img src="${u}" alt="">
            </div>`).join('');
        strip.style.display = 'flex';
    } else {
        strip.innerHTML = '';
        strip.style.display = 'none';
    }

    // Counter
    document.getElementById('lbImgCounter').textContent =
        hasImgs ? (lbCurrentIdx+1)+' dari '+e.dataUrls.length+' foto' : '0 foto';

    // Actions
    const actEl = document.getElementById('lbActions');
    const isPub = e.status === 'published';
    actEl.innerHTML = `
        <button class="lightbox-action-btn lba-edit" onclick="openGalEditModal(${e.id})">
            <svg width="13" height="13" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M11 4H4a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v14a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h14a2 2 0 0 0 2-2v-7"/><path d="M18.5 2.5a2.121 2.121 0 0 1 3 3L12 15l-4 1 1-4 9.5-9.5z"/></svg>
            Edit Informasi
        </button>
        ${!isPub ? `<button class="lightbox-action-btn lba-pub" onclick="publishGalFromDraft(${e.id});renderLightbox()">
            <svg width="13" height="13" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12"/></svg>
            Terbitkan ke Galeri
        </button>` : ''}
        <button class="lightbox-action-btn lba-del" onclick="openGalDeleteModal(${e.id})">
            <svg width="13" height="13" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><polyline points="3 6 5 6 21 6"/><path d="M19 6l-1 14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H8a2 2 0 0 1-2-2L5 6"/></svg>
            Hapus Entri
        </button>`;
}

function lbNav(dir) {
    const e = lbCurrentEntry; if(!e || e.dataUrls.length === 0) return;
    lbCurrentIdx = (lbCurrentIdx + dir + e.dataUrls.length) % e.dataUrls.length;
    renderLightbox();
}

function lbGoTo(idx) {
    lbCurrentIdx = idx;
    renderLightbox();
}

// Keyboard nav for lightbox
document.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
    if (!document.getElementById('galLightbox').classList.contains('open')) return;
    if (e.key === 'ArrowLeft')  lbNav(-1);
    if (e.key === 'ArrowRight') lbNav(1);
    if (e.key === 'Escape')     closeLightbox();
});


// ============================================
// NAVIGASI
// ============================================
const SECTIONS = ['dashboard','artikel','galeri','komentar','foto'];

function showSection(name, btn) {
    SECTIONS.forEach(s => {
        document.getElementById('section-'+s).style.display = s === name ? 'block' : 'none';
    });
    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
    if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
    renderKomentar();
    renderFoto();
    renderDraftList();
    if (name === 'galeri') { renderGalDraftList(); renderGalPubGrid(); updateGalStats(); }
    if (window.innerWidth < 769) document.getElementById('sidebar').classList.remove('open');
}

function showSectionByName(name) {
    const btn = document.querySelector('.nav-item[data-section="'+name+'"]');
    showSection(name, btn);
}


// ============================================
// LOGOUT
// ============================================
function logout() {
    openModal('logoutModal');
    if (window.innerWidth < 769) document.getElementById('sidebar').classList.remove('open');
}
function closeLogoutModal() { closeModal('logoutModal'); }
function confirmLogout() { sessionStorage.clear(); window.location.replace('login.html'); }


// ============================================
// INIT
// ============================================
renderKomentar();
renderFoto();
renderDraftList();
renderGalDraftList();
renderGalPubGrid();
updateGalStats();
// Set default date to today
document.getElementById('galTglKegiatan').valueAsDate = new Date();
</script>
</body>
</html>

CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS db_rumah_kebangsaan
    CHARACTER SET utf8mb4
    COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

USE db_rumah_kebangsaan;

SET FOREIGN_KEY_CHECKS = 0;

CREATE TABLE peran (
    id_peran    INT          AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    kode_peran  VARCHAR(50)  NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    nama_peran  VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    deskripsi   VARCHAR(255)
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE pengguna (
    id_pengguna     INT          AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    id_peran        INT          NOT NULL,
    nama_lengkap    VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    username        VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    email           VARCHAR(150) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    kata_sandi      VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    status_aktif    TINYINT(1)   DEFAULT 1,
    login_terakhir  TIMESTAMP    NULL,
    dibuat_pada     TIMESTAMP    DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    diperbarui_pada TIMESTAMP    DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (id_peran) REFERENCES peran(id_peran) ON DELETE RESTRICT
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE token_reset_sandi (
    id_token    INT          AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    id_pengguna INT          NOT NULL,
    token       VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    kadaluarsa  TIMESTAMP    NOT NULL,
    digunakan   TINYINT(1)   DEFAULT 0,
    dibuat_pada TIMESTAMP    DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (id_pengguna) REFERENCES pengguna(id_pengguna) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE berkas_file (
    id_file        INT          AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    id_pengunggah  INT          NULL,
    nama_file      VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    path_file      VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    ekstensi       VARCHAR(10)  NOT NULL,
    ukuran         BIGINT       NOT NULL,               -- [FIX] INT → BIGINT
    dibuat_pada    TIMESTAMP    DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (id_pengunggah) REFERENCES pengguna(id_pengguna) ON DELETE SET NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE kategori_artikel (
    id_kategori   INT          AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    nama_kategori VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    slug          VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    dibuat_pada   TIMESTAMP    DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE artikel (
    id_artikel        INT          AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    id_penulis        INT          NOT NULL,
    id_kategori       INT          NOT NULL,
    id_gambar_sampul  INT          NULL,
    judul             VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    slug              VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    isi_konten        TEXT         NOT NULL,
    meta_deskripsi    VARCHAR(160) NULL,
    jumlah_tayangan   INT          DEFAULT 0,         
    status_publikasi  ENUM('draft', 'terbit', 'arsip') DEFAULT 'draft',
    waktu_tayang      TIMESTAMP    NULL,
    dibuat_pada       TIMESTAMP    DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    diperbarui_pada   TIMESTAMP    DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (id_penulis)       REFERENCES pengguna(id_pengguna)         ON DELETE RESTRICT,
    FOREIGN KEY (id_kategori)      REFERENCES kategori_artikel(id_kategori) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
    FOREIGN KEY (id_gambar_sampul) REFERENCES berkas_file(id_file)          ON DELETE SET NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE galeri (
    id_galeri   INT          AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    id_file     INT          NOT NULL,
    keterangan  VARCHAR(255),
    dibuat_pada TIMESTAMP    DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (id_file) REFERENCES berkas_file(id_file) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE komentar (
    id_komentar    INT          AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    id_artikel     INT          NOT NULL,
    id_pengguna    INT          NULL,
    nama_tamu      VARCHAR(100) NULL,
    email_tamu     VARCHAR(150) NULL,
    isi_komentar   TEXT         NOT NULL,
    status_tampil  ENUM('pending', 'approved', 'rejected') DEFAULT 'pending',
    id_moderator   INT          NULL,
    waktu_moderasi TIMESTAMP    NULL,
    dibuat_pada    TIMESTAMP    DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (id_artikel)   REFERENCES artikel(id_artikel)    ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (id_pengguna)  REFERENCES pengguna(id_pengguna)  ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (id_moderator) REFERENCES pengguna(id_pengguna)  ON DELETE SET NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE foto_tamu (
    id_foto_tamu   INT          AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    id_file        INT          NOT NULL,
    nama_tamu      VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    email_tamu     VARCHAR(150) NULL,
    keterangan     VARCHAR(255),
    status_tampil  ENUM('pending', 'approved', 'rejected') DEFAULT 'pending',
    id_moderator   INT          NULL,
    waktu_moderasi TIMESTAMP    NULL,
    dicatat_pada   TIMESTAMP    DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (id_file)      REFERENCES berkas_file(id_file)  ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (id_moderator) REFERENCES pengguna(id_pengguna) ON DELETE SET NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE ulasan (
    id_ulasan     INT          AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    nama_tamu     VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    isi_ulasan    TEXT         NOT NULL,
    status_tampil ENUM('pending', 'approved', 'rejected') DEFAULT 'pending',
    id_moderator  INT          NULL,
    dibuat_pada   TIMESTAMP    DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (id_moderator) REFERENCES pengguna(id_pengguna) ON DELETE SET NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE log_aktivitas (
    id_log          INT          AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    id_pengguna     INT          NULL,
    jenis_aktivitas VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    deskripsi       TEXT         NOT NULL,
    ip_address      VARCHAR(45)  NOT NULL,
    user_agent      VARCHAR(255) NULL,
    dicatat_pada    TIMESTAMP    DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (id_pengguna) REFERENCES pengguna(id_pengguna) ON DELETE SET NULL  -- [FIX]
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE pengaturan_sistem (
    kunci           VARCHAR(100) PRIMARY KEY,
    nilai           TEXT         NOT NULL,
    deskripsi       VARCHAR(255) NULL,
    diperbarui_pada TIMESTAMP    DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
) ENGINE=InnoDB;

SET FOREIGN_KEY_CHECKS = 1;

ALTER TABLE artikel
    ADD INDEX idx_artikel_status_waktu (status_publikasi, waktu_tayang),
    ADD INDEX idx_artikel_penulis      (id_penulis),
    ADD INDEX idx_artikel_kategori     (id_kategori);

ALTER TABLE komentar
    ADD INDEX idx_komentar_artikel_status (id_artikel, status_tampil);

ALTER TABLE log_aktivitas
    ADD INDEX idx_log_pengguna_waktu (id_pengguna, dicatat_pada);

ALTER TABLE token_reset_sandi
    ADD INDEX idx_token_kadaluarsa (kadaluarsa);

        <span class="category-badge">Berita Daerah</span>
        <h1 class="article-title">Hadiri Buka Bersama Lintas Elemen, Bupati Ipuk Panen Apresiasi</h1>

        <div class="article-meta">
            <div class="meta-item">
                <svg width="18" height="18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                    <path d="M20 21v-2a4 4 0 0 0-4-4H8a4 4 0 0 0-4 4v2"></path>
                    <circle cx="12" cy="7" r="4"></circle>
                </svg>
                <strong style="color: var(--dark);">Aflahul Abidin</strong>
            </div>
            <div class="meta-item">
                <svg width="18" height="18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                    <rect x="3" y="4" width="18" height="18" rx="2" ry="2"></rect>
                    <line x1="16" y1="2" x2="16" y2="6"></line>
                    <line x1="8" y1="2" x2="8" y2="6"></line>
                    <line x1="3" y1="10" x2="21" y2="10"></line>
                </svg>
                27 Februari 2026
            </div>
            <div class="meta-item">
                <svg width="18" height="18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                    <path d="M21 10c0 7-9 13-9 13s-9-6-9-13a9 9 0 0 1 18 0z"></path>
                    <circle cx="12" cy="10" r="3"></circle>
                </svg>
                Karangrejo, Banyuwangi
            </div>
        </div>
    </header>

    <div class="main-grid">
        <article class="article-content">
            <div class="featured-image-wrapper">
                <img src="images/berita-2.png" alt="Bupati Ipuk di Rumah Kebangsaan" class="featured-image">
                <p class="image-caption">Bupati Ipuk Fiestiandani saat berdialog gayeng bersama tokoh lintas elemen di Rumah Kebangsaan Banyuwangi.</p>
            </div>

            <div class="article-body">
                <p><strong>TRIBUNJATIMTIMUR.COM, Banyuwangi</strong> &mdash; Kehadiran Bupati Banyuwangi Ipuk Fiestiandani beserta jajarannya dalam buka bersama tokoh lintas elemen di Rumah Kebangsaan asuhan jurnalis senior Hakim Said di Karangrejo, Banyuwangi, Kamis (26/02/2026) mendapat banyak apresiasi. Kehadirannya untuk berdialog dan berbaur secara gayeng dinilai sebagai sosok pemimpin yang terbuka.</p>

                <p>Bupati Ipuk duduk bersama dengan lebih dari seratus tokoh lintas elemen. Mulai dari agamawan, pejabat, pegiat sosial, kalangan pendidik, tokoh perempuan, pers, LSM hingga budayawan. Tak sedikit di antara para tokoh yang hadir adalah pihak yang kerap mengkritisi sejumlah kebijakan Pemkab Banyuwangi.</p>

                <div class="quote-box">
                    <p class="quote-text">&ldquo;Saya bersyukur bisa berdialog langsung dengan Bupati seperti ini. Berbagai persoalan yang selama tak terselesaikan bisa didialogkan dengan baik,&rdquo;</p>
                    <span class="quote-author">&mdash; Herman Sjahthi (Akademisi &amp; Aktivis Sosial)</span>
                </div>

                <p>Hal yang sama juga diungkapkan oleh Andi Purnama. Podcaster yang sering mengangkat isu-isu kebijakan publik tersebut, menilai ruang dialog yang egaliter demikian, memberikan kesan positif. &ldquo;Ada pertukaran perspektif dan pemikiran di antara kami yang kemudian melahirkan saling kepahaman. Jadi, tidak lagi hanya satu sisi dalam melihat sebuah peristiwa,&rdquo; paparnya.</p>

                <h2 class="sub-heading">Karakter Kepemimpinan yang Berani</h2>

                <p>KH. Achmad Wahyudi yang didapuk memberikan tausiyah dalam kesempatan tersebut menyebutkan jika keberanian seorang pemimpin dalam menghadapi persoalan dan menyelesaikannya adalah bentuk karakter kepemimpinan yang baik.</p>

                <div class="quote-box">
                    <p class="quote-text">&ldquo;Kita lihat saat ini, bagaimana Ibu Ipuk menjelaskan soal tambang, infrastruktur jalan, hingga layanan publik seperti ini, adalah sebuah keberanian dari seorang pemimpin. Hadir langsung dan menuntaskan persoalan merupakan karakter yang baik.&rdquo;</p>
                    <span class="quote-author">&mdash; KH. Achmad Wahyudi (Pengasuh PP. Adzikra)</span>
                </div>

                <h2 class="sub-heading">Semangat Sinergi 3KO</h2>

                <p>Ketua Rumah Kebangsaan Banyuwangi, Hakim Said, menyampaikan bahwa kegiatan ini mengusung semangat sinergitas <strong>3KO (Komunikasi, Koordinasi, dan Kolaborasi)</strong> sebagai fondasi membangun daerah. Menurutnya, forum ini menjadi ruang mempererat ukhuwah Ramadhan sekaligus memperkuat kolaborasi pemerintah dan masyarakat dalam mendukung Gerakan Nasional Indonesia ASRI (Aman, Sehat, Resik, dan Indah).</p>

                <p>&ldquo;Ini waktunya kita tandang bareng untuk mewujudkan Banyuwangi yang asri,&rdquo; tegas jurnalis senior tersebut.</p>

                <p>Sementara itu, Bupati Ipuk menyampaikan bahwa kritik terhadap pemerintah merupakan bentuk kepedulian masyarakat. &ldquo;Ketika ada kritik kepada Pemerintah Kabupaten Banyuwangi, itu adalah bukti kecintaan masyarakat dan kepedulian terhadap pemerintah,&rdquo; ujarnya.</p>

                <p>Ia mengingatkan bahwa Pemkab Banyuwangi membuka ruang pengawasan publik, namun seluruh pihak tetap harus berjalan dalam koridor aturan. &ldquo;Kami tidak menghalangi masyarakat untuk memantau pemerintah. Tetapi jangan pula menggoda pemerintah untuk tidak taat pada aturan,&rdquo; pungkasnya.</p>
            </div>
        </article>

            <button type="button" class="btn" style="border:1.5px solid var(--border);background:var(--white);color:var(--gray);font-size:.82rem;padding:.5rem 1rem" onclick="closeCaptchaModal()">Batal</button>
            <button type="button" class="btn btn-primary" style="font-size:.82rem;padding:.5rem 1rem" id="btnConfirmCaptcha" onclick="confirmCaptcha()">Verifikasi</button>
        </div>
    </div>

<script>
// ============================================
// AUTH & NAVIGASI
// ============================================
const isLoggedIn = () => sessionStorage.getItem('rk_logged_in') === 'true';

function updateNav() {
    const mainBtn = document.getElementById('mainLoginBtn');
    const mobBtn  = document.getElementById('mobLoginBtn');

    if (isLoggedIn()) {
        const role   = sessionStorage.getItem('rk_role');
        const target = (role === 'superadmin') ? 'superadmin.html' : 'admin.html';
        if (mainBtn) { mainBtn.textContent = 'Dashboard'; mainBtn.href = target; }
        if (mobBtn)  { mobBtn.textContent  = 'Dashboard'; mobBtn.href  = target; }
    } else {
        if (mainBtn) { mainBtn.textContent = 'Login'; mainBtn.href = 'login.html'; }
        if (mobBtn)  { mobBtn.textContent  = 'Login'; mobBtn.href  = 'login.html'; }
    }
}
updateNav();

function requireLogin() {
    if (!isLoggedIn()) {
        window.location.href = 'login.html';
        return false;
    }
    return true;
}

// ============================================
// NAVBAR & MOBILE MENU
// ============================================
window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
    document.getElementById('navbar').classList.toggle('scrolled', window.scrollY > 50);
});

function openMobMenu() {
    document.getElementById('mobMenu').classList.add('open');
    document.getElementById('mobOverlay').classList.add('open');
}
function closeMobMenu() {
    document.getElementById('mobMenu').classList.remove('open');
    document.getElementById('mobOverlay').classList.remove('open');
}
document.getElementById('mobileToggle').addEventListener('click', openMobMenu);
document.getElementById('mobClose').addEventListener('click', closeMobMenu);
document.getElementById('mobOverlay').addEventListener('click', closeMobMenu);
document.querySelectorAll('.mob-nav-link').forEach(l => l.addEventListener('click', closeMobMenu));

// ============================================
// FILTER KATA KASAR
// ============================================
const KASAR_WORDS = ['bajingan','brengsek','keparat','bangsat','anjing','babi','tolol','goblok','idiot'];
const KASAR_REGEX = new RegExp('\\b(' + KASAR_WORDS.join('|') + ')\\b', 'gi');
function adaKasar(teks) { KASAR_REGEX.lastIndex = 0; return KASAR_REGEX.test(teks); }

// ============================================
// MODAL CAPTCHA
// ============================================
let pendingSubmitAction = null;
let isModalCaptchaChecked = false;

function toggleModalCaptcha() {
    isModalCaptchaChecked = !isModalCaptchaChecked;
    document.getElementById('modalCaptchaCheck').classList.toggle('checked', isModalCaptchaChecked);
}

function openCaptchaModal(actionCallback) {
    pendingSubmitAction = actionCallback;
    isModalCaptchaChecked = false;
    document.getElementById('modalCaptchaCheck').classList.remove('checked');
    document.getElementById('captchaModal').classList.add('open');
}

function closeCaptchaModal() {
    pendingSubmitAction = null;
    document.getElementById('captchaModal').classList.remove('open');
}

function confirmCaptcha() {
    if (!isModalCaptchaChecked) { showToast('Centang verifikasi terlebih dahulu.', 'warning'); return; }
    closeCaptchaModal();
    if (pendingSubmitAction) pendingSubmitAction();
}

// Close modal on backdrop click
document.getElementById('captchaModal').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    if (e.target === this) closeCaptchaModal();
});

// ============================================
// KOMENTAR
// ============================================
function kirimKomentar(id) {
    if (!requireLogin()) return;

    const nama = document.getElementById('cn-' + id).value.trim();
    const teks = document.getElementById('ct-' + id).value.trim();

    if (!nama || !teks) { showToast('Nama dan komentar wajib diisi.', 'warning'); return; }
    if (adaKasar(teks)) { showToast('Komentar mengandung kata yang tidak pantas.', 'error'); return; }

    openCaptchaModal(() => {
        const list = document.getElementById('cmts-' + id);
        const el   = document.createElement('div');
        el.className   = 'comment-pending';
        el.textContent = 'Komentar Anda sedang menunggu persetujuan admin.';
        list.appendChild(el);

        const cntEl = document.getElementById('cnt-' + id);
        if (cntEl) cntEl.textContent = parseInt(cntEl.textContent) + 1;

        document.getElementById('cn-' + id).value = '';
        document.getElementById('ct-' + id).value = '';
        showToast('Komentar terkirim. Menunggu moderasi admin.', 'success');
    });
}

// ============================================
// TESTIMONI
// ============================================
document.getElementById('formTestimoni').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!requireLogin()) return;

    const nama  = document.getElementById('testiNama').value.trim();
    const pesan = document.getElementById('testiPesan').value.trim();

    if (!nama || !pesan) { showToast('Lengkapi semua kolom terlebih dahulu.', 'warning'); return; }
    if (adaKasar(pesan)) { showToast('Pesan mengandung kata yang tidak pantas.', 'error'); return; }

    openCaptchaModal(() => {
        this.reset();
        showToast('Ulasan dikirim. Menunggu moderasi admin.', 'success');
    });
});

// ============================================
// UPLOAD FOTO
// ============================================
const ALLOWED_TYPES = ['image/jpeg','image/jpg','image/png','image/webp'];
const MAX_SIZE = 5 * 1024 * 1024;

document.getElementById('fotoFile').addEventListener('change', function() {
    const f   = this.files[0];
    const err = document.getElementById('fileErr');
    const txt = document.getElementById('fileTxt');
    const box = document.getElementById('fileBox');

    if (!f) return;

    if (!ALLOWED_TYPES.includes(f.type) || f.size > MAX_SIZE) {
        err.textContent = !ALLOWED_TYPES.includes(f.type)
            ? 'Format tidak didukung. Gunakan JPG, PNG, atau WEBP.'
            : 'Ukuran file melebihi batas 5MB.';
        err.classList.add('show');
        box.style.borderColor = 'var(--primary)';
        this.value = '';
        return;
    }

    err.classList.remove('show');
    box.style.borderColor = '#15803D';
    txt.textContent = f.name.substring(0, 28) + (f.name.length > 28 ? '...' : '') + ' dipilih';
});

document.getElementById('formFoto').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!requireLogin()) return;

    const nama = document.getElementById('fotoNama').value.trim();
    const file = document.getElementById('fotoFile').files[0];

    if (!nama) { showToast('Nama pengunjung wajib diisi.', 'warning'); return; }
    if (!file) { showToast('Pilih foto terlebih dahulu.', 'warning'); return; }

    openCaptchaModal(() => {
        this.reset();
        document.getElementById('fileTxt').textContent = 'Klik untuk pilih foto';
        document.getElementById('fileBox').style.borderColor = '';
        document.getElementById('fileErr').classList.remove('show');
        showToast('Foto berhasil diunggah. Menunggu moderasi admin.', 'success');
    });
});

// ============================================
// ANIMASI REVEAL & TOAST
// ============================================
const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
    (entries) => entries.forEach(e => { if (e.isIntersecting) e.target.classList.add('active'); }),
    { threshold: 0.1 }
);
document.querySelectorAll('.reveal').forEach(el => observer.observe(el));

function showToast(msg, type = 'success') {
    const t = document.getElementById('toast');
    t.textContent = msg;
    t.className = 'toast ' + type + ' show';
    setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 3500);
}
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
// ============================================
// AKUN TERDAFTAR
// ============================================
const ACCOUNTS = [
    { username: 'superadmin',               password: 'super123',  role: 'superadmin', redirect: 'superadmin.html' },
    { username: 'admin',                    password: 'admin123',  role: 'admin',      redirect: 'admin.html' },
    { username: 'hakim@rumahkebangsaan.id', password: 'hakim123',  role: 'admin',      redirect: 'admin.html' },
    { username: 'developer@poli.edu',       password: 'dev123',    role: 'superadmin', redirect: 'superadmin.html' },
];

// Restore "remember me"
(function restoreRemember() {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem('rk_remember');
    if (saved) {
        document.getElementById('username').value = saved;
        document.getElementById('rememberMe').checked = true;
    }
})();

// ============================================
// TOGGLE PASSWORD
// ============================================
document.getElementById('togglePw').addEventListener('click', function() {
    const pw   = document.getElementById('password');
    const show = pw.type === 'password';
    pw.type          = show ? 'text' : 'password';
    this.textContent = show ? 'SEMBUNYIKAN' : 'LIHAT';
});

// ============================================
// SUBMIT LOGIN
// ============================================
document.getElementById('loginForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();

    const uname    = document.getElementById('username').value.trim();
    const pass     = document.getElementById('password').value;
    const remember = document.getElementById('rememberMe').checked;
    const errorBox = document.getElementById('errorBox');
    const errorMsg = document.getElementById('errorMsg');
    const btn      = document.getElementById('loginBtn');

    // Reset error state
    errorBox.classList.remove('show');
    document.getElementById('username').classList.remove('error');
    document.getElementById('password').classList.remove('error');

    // Validasi kosong
    if (!uname || !pass) {
        errorMsg.textContent = 'Email atau username dan kata sandi wajib diisi.';
        errorBox.classList.add('show');
        if (!uname) document.getElementById('username').classList.add('error');
        if (!pass)  document.getElementById('password').classList.add('error');
        return;
    }

    // Loading state
    btn.classList.add('loading');
    btn.disabled = true;

    setTimeout(() => {
        const acc = ACCOUNTS.find(a => a.username === uname && a.password === pass);

        btn.classList.remove('loading');
        btn.disabled = false;

        if (acc) {
            sessionStorage.setItem('rk_logged_in', 'true');
            sessionStorage.setItem('rk_role',      acc.role);
            sessionStorage.setItem('rk_username',  acc.username);

            if (remember) {
                localStorage.setItem('rk_remember', uname);
            } else {
                localStorage.removeItem('rk_remember');
            }

            window.location.href = acc.redirect;
        } else {
            errorMsg.textContent = 'Kredensial yang Anda masukkan tidak cocok dengan catatan kami.';
            errorBox.classList.add('show');
            document.getElementById('username').classList.add('error');
            document.getElementById('password').classList.add('error');
            document.getElementById('password').value = '';
            document.getElementById('password').focus();
        }
    }, 800);
});

// function showForgot(e) {
//     e.preventDefault();
//     alert('Hubungi tim IT / Administrator Sistem untuk mereset kata sandi Anda:\ndeveloper@poli.edu');
// }
</script>
</body>
</html>

                <input class="obox" type="text" maxlength="1" inputmode="numeric" id="o3">
                <input class="obox" type="text" maxlength="1" inputmode="numeric" id="o4">
                <input class="obox" type="text" maxlength="1" inputmode="numeric" id="o5">
            </div>

            <button class="btn" id="btnVerify" onclick="verifyOtp()" disabled>
                <div class="spin" id="spVerify"></div>
                <span>Verifikasi Kode</span>
                <svg id="icVerify" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12"/></svg>

            <div class="resend-row">

                Ganti email

                <span id="altPassMsg">Password tidak cocok.</span>

            <div class="fgroup">
                <label class="flabel" for="newPass">Password Baru</label>

                    <svg class="iicon" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><rect x="3" y="11" width="18" height="11" rx="2"/><path d="M7 11V7a5 5 0 0110 0v4"/></svg>
                    <button type="button" class="ptoggle" onclick="togglePw('newPass',this)" tabindex="-1">LIHAT</button>
                </div>
                <div class="sbar"><div class="sseg" id="s1"></div><div class="sseg" id="s2"></div><div class="sseg" id="s3"></div><div class="sseg" id="s4"></div></div>

                    <svg class="iicon" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><rect x="3" y="11" width="18" height="11" rx="2"/><path d="M7 11V7a5 5 0 0110 0v4"/></svg>
                    <button type="button" class="ptoggle" onclick="togglePw('confPass',this)" tabindex="-1">LIHAT</button>

<script>
    let step = 1, email = '', otp = '', cdInt = null;

    function goTo(n) {
        document.querySelector('.panel.active')?.classList.remove('active');
        document.getElementById('panel' + n).classList.add('active');
        step = n;
        updateLeft(n);
    }

    function updateLeft(active) {
        for (let i = 1; i <= 3; i++) {
            const row = document.getElementById('si' + i);
            const dot = document.getElementById('sn' + i);
            row.className = 'step-item' +
                (i < active ? ' is-done' : i === active ? ' is-active' : '');
            dot.textContent = i < active ? '✓' : i;
        }
    }

    function sendOtp() {
        const el  = document.getElementById('emailInput');
        const val = el.value.trim();
        const err = document.getElementById('emailErr');
        const alt = document.getElementById('altEmail');

        el.classList.remove('bad');
        err.style.display = 'none';
        alt.classList.remove('show');

        if (!val || !/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(val)) {
            el.classList.add('bad'); err.style.display = 'block'; return;
        }

        load('btnSend','spSend','icSend','lblSend', true, 'Mengirim...');

        setTimeout(() => {
            load('btnSend','spSend','icSend','lblSend', false, 'Kirim Kode Verifikasi');

            if (val.toLowerCase() === 'gagal@test.com') {
                document.getElementById('altEmailMsg').textContent = 'Email tidak terdaftar.';
                alt.classList.add('show'); return;
            }

            email = val;
            otp   = String(Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000));
            console.info('%c[PROTOTYPE] OTP: ' + otp, 'color:#B91C1C;font-weight:700;font-size:14px');

            document.getElementById('emailDisplay').textContent = mask(val);
            goTo(2); initOtp(); startCd();
        }, 1400);
    }

    function initOtp() {
        const boxes = Array.from({length:6}, (_,i) => document.getElementById('o'+i));
        boxes.forEach((b, i) => {
            b.value = ''; b.classList.remove('on');
            b.oninput = null; b.onkeydown = null; b.onpaste = null;

            b.addEventListener('input', e => {
                const v = e.target.value.replace(/\D/g,'');
                b.value = v ? v.slice(-1) : '';
                b.classList.toggle('on', !!b.value);
                if (b.value && i < 5) boxes[i+1].focus();
                chkOtp(boxes);
            });

            b.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
                if (e.key === 'Backspace' && !b.value && i > 0) {
                    boxes[i-1].value = ''; boxes[i-1].classList.remove('on');
                    boxes[i-1].focus(); chkOtp(boxes);
                }
            });

            b.addEventListener('paste', e => {
                e.preventDefault();
                const p = (e.clipboardData||window.clipboardData).getData('text').replace(/\D/g,'');
                p.split('').slice(0,6).forEach((c,j) => {
                    if(boxes[j]) { boxes[j].value=c; boxes[j].classList.add('on'); }
                });
                chkOtp(boxes);
                (boxes[Math.min(p.length,5)]||boxes[5]).focus();
            });
        });
        boxes[0].focus();
    }

    function chkOtp(boxes) {
        document.getElementById('btnVerify').disabled = !boxes.every(b => b.value);
    }

    function verifyOtp() {
        const boxes = Array.from({length:6}, (_,i) => document.getElementById('o'+i));
        const entered = boxes.map(b => b.value).join('');
        const alt = document.getElementById('altOtp');
        alt.classList.remove('show');

        load('btnVerify','spVerify','icVerify',null, true);

        setTimeout(() => {
            load('btnVerify','spVerify','icVerify',null, false);

            if (entered !== otp) {
                document.getElementById('altOtpMsg').textContent = 'Kode salah. Periksa inbox email Anda.';
                alt.classList.add('show');
                boxes.forEach(b => { b.value=''; b.classList.remove('on'); });
                boxes[0].focus(); chkOtp(boxes); return;
            }

            clearInterval(cdInt);
            goTo(3);
        }, 1100);
    }

    function startCd() {
        let s = 60;
        const cdEl = document.getElementById('cd');
        const wrap = document.getElementById('cdWrap');
        const btn  = document.getElementById('resendBtn');
        btn.disabled = true; wrap.style.display = '';
        clearInterval(cdInt);
        cdInt = setInterval(() => {
            s--; cdEl.textContent = s;
            if (s <= 0) {
                clearInterval(cdInt);
                btn.disabled = false;
                wrap.style.display = 'none';
                btn.innerHTML = 'Kirim ulang kode';
            }
        }, 1000);
    }

    function resendOtp() {
        otp = String(Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000));
        console.info('%c[PROTOTYPE] OTP baru: ' + otp, 'color:#B91C1C;font-weight:700;font-size:14px');
        toast('✓ Kode baru dikirim ke ' + mask(email));
        document.getElementById('resendBtn').innerHTML =
            'Kirim ulang <span id="cdWrap">(<span id="cd">60</span>s)</span>';
        startCd();
        const boxes = Array.from({length:6},(_,i)=>document.getElementById('o'+i));
        boxes.forEach(b=>{b.value='';b.classList.remove('on');});
        document.getElementById('altOtp').classList.remove('show');
        boxes[0].focus(); chkOtp(boxes);
    }

    function chkStrength(v) {
        const cols = ['','#EF4444','#F97316','#EAB308','#22C55E'];
        const labs = ['Masukkan password','Lemah','Cukup','Kuat','Sangat Kuat'];
        let score = 0;
        if (v.length >= 8)                         score++;
        if (/[A-Z]/.test(v) && /[a-z]/.test(v))   score++;
        if (/\d/.test(v))                           score++;
        if (/[^A-Za-z0-9]/.test(v))                score++;
        for (let i=1;i<=4;i++) {
            document.getElementById('s'+i).style.background = i<=score ? cols[score] : 'var(--border)';
        }
        const lbl = document.getElementById('slbl');
        lbl.textContent = labs[v ? score : 0];
        lbl.style.color = v ? (cols[score]||'var(--muted)') : 'var(--muted)';
    }

    function doReset() {
        const np = document.getElementById('newPass').value;
        const cp = document.getElementById('confPass').value;
        const alt = document.getElementById('altPass');
        const ce  = document.getElementById('confErr');

        alt.classList.remove('show'); ce.style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('newPass').classList.remove('bad');
        document.getElementById('confPass').classList.remove('bad');

        if (np.length < 8) {
            document.getElementById('altPassMsg').textContent = 'Password minimal 8 karakter.';
            alt.classList.add('show');
            document.getElementById('newPass').classList.add('bad'); return;
        }
        if (np !== cp) {
            ce.style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('confPass').classList.add('bad'); return;
        }

        load('btnReset','spReset','icReset',null, true);
        setTimeout(() => { load('btnReset','spReset','icReset',null,false); goTo(4); }, 1400);
    }

    function togglePw(id, btn) {
        const inp = document.getElementById(id);
        const show = inp.type === 'password';
        inp.type = show ? 'text' : 'password';
        btn.textContent = show ? 'SEMBUNYIKAN' : 'LIHAT';
    }

    function load(btnId, spId, icId, lblId, on, lbl) {
        const btn = document.getElementById(btnId);
        const sp  = document.getElementById(spId);
        const ic  = icId  ? document.getElementById(icId)  : null;
        const lb  = lblId ? document.getElementById(lblId) : null;
        btn.disabled = on;
        sp.style.display = on ? 'block' : 'none';
        if (ic) ic.style.display = on ? 'none' : '';
        if (lb && on && lbl) lb.textContent = lbl;
        if (lb && !on && lbl) lb.textContent = lbl;
    }

    function mask(e) {
        const [u,d] = e.split('@');
        return u[0]+'*'.repeat(Math.max(1,u.length-2))+u.slice(-1)+'@'+d;
    }

    function toast(msg) {
        const t = document.getElementById('toast');
        t.textContent = msg; t.classList.add('show');
        setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 3200);
    }

    document.getElementById('emailInput').addEventListener('keydown', e => {
        if (e.key === 'Enter') sendOtp();
    });
</script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        // ============================================
        // TOGGLE PASSWORD
        // ============================================
        function setupToggle(inputId, btnId) {
            const input = document.getElementById(inputId);
            const btn   = document.getElementById(btnId);
            btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                const show      = input.type === 'password';
                input.type      = show ? 'text' : 'password';
                btn.textContent = show ? 'SEMBUNYIKAN' : 'LIHAT';
            });
        }

        setupToggle('regPassword', 'togglePw1');
        setupToggle('regConfirm',  'togglePw2');

        // ============================================
        // PASSWORD STRENGTH
        // ============================================
        document.getElementById('regPassword').addEventListener('input', function() {
            const val   = this.value;
            const wrap  = document.getElementById('strengthWrap');
            const fill  = document.getElementById('strengthFill');
            const label = document.getElementById('strengthLabel');

            if (!val) {
                wrap.classList.remove('show');
                fill.style.width = '0%';
                label.textContent = '';
                updateConfirmHint();
                return;
            }

            wrap.classList.add('show');

            let score = 0;
            if (val.length >= 8)          score++;
            if (/[A-Z]/.test(val))        score++;
            if (/[0-9]/.test(val))        score++;
            if (/[^A-Za-z0-9]/.test(val)) score++;

            const levels = [
                { pct: '25%', color: '#EF4444', text: 'Lemah' },
                { pct: '50%', color: '#F97316', text: 'Cukup' },
                { pct: '75%', color: '#EAB308', text: 'Kuat' },
                { pct: '100%', color: '#16A34A', text: 'Sangat Kuat' },
            ];

            const lvl = levels[Math.max(0, score - 1)];
            fill.style.width      = lvl.pct;
            fill.style.background = lvl.color;
            label.textContent     = 'Kekuatan: ' + lvl.text;
            label.style.color     = lvl.color;

            updateConfirmHint();
        });

        // ============================================
        // CONFIRM PASSWORD
        // ============================================
        function updateConfirmHint() {
            const pass    = document.getElementById('regPassword').value;
            const confirm = document.getElementById('regConfirm').value;
            const hint    = document.getElementById('hintConfirm');
            const input   = document.getElementById('regConfirm');

            if (!confirm) {
                hint.classList.remove('show', 'error', 'success');
                input.classList.remove('error', 'valid');
                return;
            }

            if (pass === confirm) {
                hint.textContent = '\u2713 Kata sandi cocok';
                hint.className   = 'field-hint show success';
                input.classList.remove('error');
                input.classList.add('valid');
            } else {
                hint.textContent = '\u2717 Kata sandi tidak cocok';
                hint.className   = 'field-hint show error';
                input.classList.remove('valid');
                input.classList.add('error');
            }
        }

        document.getElementById('regConfirm').addEventListener('input', updateConfirmHint);

        // ============================================
        // HELPER: setField
        // ============================================
        function setField(inputId, hintId, isValid, msg) {
            const input = document.getElementById(inputId);
            const hint  = document.getElementById(hintId);

            if (isValid) {
                input.classList.remove('error');
                input.classList.add('valid');
                hint.textContent = '';
                hint.classList.remove('show');
            } else {
                input.classList.add('error');
                input.classList.remove('valid');
                hint.textContent = msg;
                hint.className   = 'field-hint show error';
            }

            return isValid;
        }

        // ============================================
        // FORM SUBMIT
        // ============================================
        document.getElementById('registerForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();

            const nama     = document.getElementById('regNama').value.trim();
            const email    = document.getElementById('regEmail').value.trim();
            const password = document.getElementById('regPassword').value;
            const confirm  = document.getElementById('regConfirm').value;

            const results = [
                setField('regNama',     'hintNama',     nama.length >= 3,                                  'Nama minimal 3 karakter.'),
                setField('regEmail',    'hintEmail',    /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email),          'Format email tidak valid.'),
                setField('regPassword', 'hintPassword', password.length >= 8,                              'Kata sandi minimal 8 karakter.'),
                setField('regConfirm',  'hintConfirm',  password === confirm && confirm.length > 0,        'Konfirmasi kata sandi tidak cocok.'),
            ];

            const valid = results.every(Boolean);

            if (!valid) {
                const firstErr = document.querySelector('.form-control.error');
                if (firstErr) firstErr.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                return;
            }

            const btn = document.getElementById('registerBtn');
            btn.classList.add('loading');
            btn.disabled = true;

            setTimeout(() => {
                sessionStorage.setItem('rk_registered_email', email);

                document.getElementById('registerForm').style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('formHeader').style.display   = 'none';
                document.getElementById('successCard').classList.add('show');

                btn.classList.remove('loading');
                btn.disabled = false;
            }, 1000);
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
