<script>
// ============================================
// AUTH GUARD — hanya superadmin
// ============================================
(function() {
    if (sessionStorage.getItem('rk_logged_in') !== 'true' || sessionStorage.getItem('rk_role') !== 'superadmin') {
        window.location.replace('login.html');
        return;
    }
    const u = sessionStorage.getItem('rk_username') || 'Super Admin';
    document.getElementById('uname').textContent   = u;
    document.getElementById('uavatar').textContent = u.substring(0, 2).toUpperCase();
})();

// ============================================
// DATA
// ============================================
let users = [
    { id:1, nama:'Bapak Hakim',             email:'hakim@rumahkebangsaan.id', role:'admin',      locked:false },
    { id:2, nama:'Tim IT TRPL (Jevon dkk)', email:'developer@poli.edu',       role:'superadmin', locked:true  },
    { id:3, nama:'Staf Internal',            email:'staf@rumahkebangsaan.id',  role:'admin',      locked:false },
];
let nextId = 4;

let logs = [
    { type:'danger',  title:'Akses Ditolak (Bypass URL)',  desc:'Tamu mencoba akses langsung halaman admin melalui URL.', time:'10 menit lalu' },
    { type:'success', title:'Sistem Filter Bekerja',       desc:'Menolak file .exe pada form UGC pengunjung.',            time:'1 jam lalu'    },
    { type:'success', title:'Login Berhasil',              desc:'Super Admin berhasil masuk ke sistem.',                  time:'2 jam lalu'    },
    { type:'warning', title:'Percobaan Login Gagal',       desc:'Gagal 3 kali dari IP 192.168.1.105.',                    time:'3 jam lalu'    },
];

// ============================================
// RENDER USERS
// ============================================
function renderUsers() {
    const tbody = document.getElementById('userTable');
    const prev  = document.getElementById('mainUserPrev');
    document.getElementById('userCount').textContent = users.length + ' pengguna terdaftar';
    document.getElementById('statAdmin').textContent = users.length;

    const rowMain = u => `
        <tr>
            <td>
                <div class="user-name-cell">${escHtml(u.nama)}</div>
                <div class="user-email-cell">${escHtml(u.email)}</div>
            </td>
            <td>
                <span class="role-badge ${u.role === 'superadmin' ? 'role-super' : 'role-admin'}">
                    ${u.role === 'superadmin' ? 'Super Admin' : 'Admin Konten'}
                </span>
            </td>
            <td>
                ${u.locked
                    ? `<span style="font-size:.73rem;color:var(--muted)">Terkunci</span>`
                    : `<button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm" onclick="openEditModal(${u.id})" style="margin-right:.4rem">Edit</button>
                       <button class="btn btn-danger-soft btn-sm" onclick="deleteUser(${u.id})">Hapus</button>`
                }
            </td>
        </tr>`;

    const rowPrev = u => `
        <tr>
            <td>
                <div class="user-name-cell">${escHtml(u.nama)}</div>
                <div class="user-email-cell">${escHtml(u.email)}</div>
            </td>
            <td>
                <span class="role-badge ${u.role === 'superadmin' ? 'role-super' : 'role-admin'}">
                    ${u.role === 'superadmin' ? 'Super Admin' : 'Admin'}
                </span>
            </td>
            <td><span class="status-dot"><span class="status-indicator" style="width:5px;height:5px"></span>Aktif</span></td>
        </tr>`;

    if (tbody) tbody.innerHTML = users.map(rowMain).join('');
    if (prev)  prev.innerHTML  = users.map(rowPrev).join('');
}

// ============================================
// RENDER LOGS
// ============================================
function renderLogs() {
    const bgMap    = { danger:'#FEF2F2', success:'#F0FDF4', warning:'#FFFBEB' };
    const dotMap   = { danger:'var(--danger)', success:'var(--success)', warning:'var(--warning)' };
    const labelMap = { danger:'Peringatan', success:'Berhasil', warning:'Perhatian' };

    const logHTML = items => items.map(l => `
        <div class="log-item">
            <div class="log-icon-wrap" style="background:${bgMap[l.type]||'#F5F5F4'}">
                <span style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:50%;background:${dotMap[l.type]||'#78716C'};display:inline-block"></span>
            </div>
            <div class="log-info">
                <h4>${escHtml(l.title)}</h4>
                <p>${escHtml(l.desc)}</p>
                <span class="log-time" style="color:${dotMap[l.type]||'var(--muted)'}">${labelMap[l.type]||''} &mdash; ${l.time}</span>
            </div>
        </div>`
    ).join('');

    const fl = document.getElementById('fullLog');
    const pv = document.getElementById('logPrev');
    if (fl) fl.innerHTML = logHTML(logs);
    if (pv) pv.innerHTML = logHTML(logs.slice(0, 3));
}

// ============================================
// USER CRUD
// ============================================
let editingId = null;

function openModal() {
    editingId = null;
    document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = 'Tambah Akun Admin';
    document.getElementById('mNama').value  = '';
    document.getElementById('mEmail').value = '';
    document.getElementById('mRole').value  = 'admin';
    document.getElementById('userModalOverlay').classList.add('open');
    document.getElementById('mNama').focus();
}

function openEditModal(id) {
    const u = users.find(x => x.id === id);
    if (!u) return;
    editingId = id;
    document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = 'Edit Akun: ' + u.nama;
    document.getElementById('mNama').value  = u.nama;
    document.getElementById('mEmail').value = u.email;
    document.getElementById('mRole').value  = u.role;
    document.getElementById('userModalOverlay').classList.add('open');
}

function closeModal() {
    document.getElementById('userModalOverlay').classList.remove('open');
    editingId = null;
}

document.getElementById('userModalOverlay').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    if (e.target === this) closeModal();
});

document.getElementById('modalSaveBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
    const nama  = document.getElementById('mNama').value.trim();
    const email = document.getElementById('mEmail').value.trim();
    const role  = document.getElementById('mRole').value;

    if (!nama || !email) { showToast('Nama dan email wajib diisi.', 'danger'); return; }
    if (!/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email)) { showToast('Format email tidak valid.', 'danger'); return; }

    if (editingId !== null) {
        const u = users.find(x => x.id === editingId);
        if (u) { u.nama = nama; u.email = email; u.role = role; }
        logs.unshift({ type:'success', title:'Akun Diperbarui', desc:'Akun ' + nama + ' berhasil diperbarui.', time:'Baru saja' });
        showToast('Akun ' + nama + ' berhasil diperbarui.', 'success');
    } else {
        if (users.find(u => u.email === email)) {
            showToast('Email sudah digunakan akun lain.', 'danger');
            return;
        }
        users.push({ id: nextId++, nama, email, role, locked: false });
        logs.unshift({ type:'success', title:'Pengguna Baru Ditambahkan', desc:'Akun ' + nama + ' (' + (role === 'superadmin' ? 'Super Admin' : 'Admin') + ') ditambahkan.', time:'Baru saja' });
        showToast('Akun ' + nama + ' berhasil ditambahkan.', 'success');
    }

    closeModal();
    renderUsers();
    renderLogs();
});

function deleteUser(id) {
    const u = users.find(x => x.id === id);
    if (!u) return;
    if (confirm('Hapus akses ' + u.nama + '?\nTindakan ini tidak dapat dibatalkan.')) {
        users = users.filter(x => x.id !== id);
        logs.unshift({ type:'danger', title:'Pengguna Dihapus', desc:'Akun ' + u.nama + ' dihapus dari sistem.', time:'Baru saja' });
        renderUsers();
        renderLogs();
        showToast('Akun ' + u.nama + ' dihapus.', 'danger');
    }
}

// ============================================
// NAVIGATION
// ============================================
const ALL_SECTIONS = ['main','users','logs','analitik','settings'];

function showSection(name, btn) {
    ALL_SECTIONS.forEach(s => {
        document.getElementById('section-' + s).style.display = s === name ? 'block' : 'none';
    });
    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));

    if (btn && btn.classList) {
        btn.classList.add('active');
    } else {
        const menuBtn = document.querySelector('.nav-item[data-section="' + name + '"]');
        if (menuBtn) menuBtn.classList.add('active');
    }

    renderUsers();
    renderLogs();
    if (window.innerWidth < 769) document.getElementById('sidebar').classList.remove('open');
}

function showSectionByName(name) {
    showSection(name, null);
}

// ============================================
// REAL-TIME COUNTER SIMULATION
// ============================================
setInterval(() => {
    const el = document.getElementById('activeV');
    if (el) {
        const v = parseInt(el.textContent) || 84;
        el.textContent = Math.max(50, Math.min(150, v + Math.floor(Math.random() * 7) - 3));
    }
}, 5000);

// ============================================
// LOGOUT SYSTEM
// ============================================
function logout() {
    document.getElementById('logoutModal').classList.add('open');
    if (window.innerWidth < 769) {
        document.getElementById('sidebar').classList.remove('open');
    }
}

function closeLogoutModal() {
    document.getElementById('logoutModal').classList.remove('open');
}

function confirmLogout() {
    sessionStorage.clear();
    window.location.replace('login.html');
}

document.getElementById('logoutModal').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    if (e.target === this) closeLogoutModal();
});

// ============================================
// HELPERS
// ============================================
function escHtml(str) {
    return String(str)
        .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
        .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
        .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
        .replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
}

function showToast(msg, type = 'success') {
    const t = document.getElementById('toast');
    t.textContent = msg;
    t.className = 'toast ' + type + ' show';
    setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 3500);
}

// INIT
renderUsers();
renderLogs();
</script>
</body>
</html>
